# Arquitetura do Firmware вҖ” Monitor de AquГЎrio Inteligente (DDIno)

## 1. VisГЈo Geral

Firmware bare-metal/RTOS para ESP32-S3 (N16R8) que implementa um monitor/controlador de aquГЎrio com:

- 10 tomadas inteligentes (relГ©s via MCP23017 I2C)
- Sensores: temperatura (DS18B20), nГӯvel ATO (XKC-Y25-V via ADC), corrente (ACS712 20A Г— 8 + ADC), energia (PZEM-004T v4.0)
- RTC DS3231 para timestamp
- Display TFT 480Г—320 + Touch XPT2046 + AD Keypad
- API HTTP `/api/v1` para integraГ§ГЈo LAN
- Safety pipeline com 3 FSMs + Safety Controller + Circuit Breaker + WDT

## 2. Mapa de MГіdulos

```
app_main.c  вҶҗ entry point (loop 50ms)
  в”Ӯ
  в”ңв”Җв”Җ hal/          inicializaГ§ГЈo I2C, SPI, UART
  в”ңв”Җв”Җ drivers/      acesso direto ao hardware
  в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җв”Җ driver_mcp23017    I2C: relГ©s P03-P10, buzzer, LED
  в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җв”Җ driver_relay       API uniforme P01-P10 (P01,P02 GPIO; P03-P10 MCP)
  в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җв”Җ driver_mcp3208     SPI: 2Г— MCP3208 (ADC corrente, ATO, keypad)
  в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җв”Җ driver_acs712      leitura corrente por plug
  в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җв”Җ driver_ad_keypad   decodificaГ§ГЈo teclado 5V condicionado
  в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җв”Җ driver_pzem        UART: PZEM-004T v4.0 (V, A, W, Wh, Hz, PF)
  в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җв”Җ driver_ds18b20     1-Wire bit-banged (GPIO4)
  в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җв”Җ driver_ds3231      I2C: RTC DS3231
  в”Ӯ   в””в”Җв”Җ driver_buzzer_led  LED 3 cores + buzzer via MCP23017 GPB
  в”ңв”Җв”Җ core/          lГіgica central de safety
  в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җв”Җ safety_controller  mГЎquina de estados global (NORMALвҶ’DEGRADEDвҶ’SAFE_OFFвҶ’EMERGENCY)
  в”Ӯ   в””в”Җв”Җ circuit_breaker    padrГЈo circuit breaker para cada barramento
  в”ңв”Җв”Җ fsm/           mГЎquinas de estado especializadas
  в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җв”Җ thermal_fsm    temperatura (NORMAL/ALERT/CRITICAL/EXTREME/SENSOR_FAIL)
  в”Ӯ   в””в”Җв”Җ ato_fsm        nГӯvel ATO (NORMAL/REFILLING/OVERFLOW/BLOCKED/ERROR/DISABLED)
  в”ңв”Җв”Җ services/      serviГ§os de aplicaГ§ГЈo
  в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җв”Җ command_validator   valida se um comando Г© permitido dado o estado global
  в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җв”Җ relay_safety_service bloqueia acionamento se safety violado
  в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җв”Җ alert_manager       gerenciamento de alarmes (ALM-001 a ALM-065)
  в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җв”Җ self_test           autoteste de HW na inicializaГ§ГЈo
  в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җв”Җ electric_fsm        FSM elГ©trica (NORMAL/HIGH_CONSUMPTION/OVERLOAD/SENSOR_FAIL)
  в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җв”Җ safeoff_alm_map     mapeia safeoff_reason вҶ’ ALM-ID
  в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җв”Җ cdn_energy          acumulador de energia Wh por plugue
  в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җв”Җ storage_sd          log + backup em cartГЈo SD (FATFS/SPI)
  в”Ӯ   в””в”Җв”Җ wdt_advanced        watchdog configurГЎvel por tarefa
  в”ңв”Җв”Җ web/           servidor HTTP
  в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җв”Җ api_rest         handlers + roteamento /api/v1/*
  в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җв”Җ api_auth         autenticaГ§ГЈo SHA-256 + token RAM
  в”Ӯ   в””в”Җв”Җ api_rate_limit   rate limit por IP (30 req/min)
  в”ңв”Җв”Җ ui/            interface LVGL
  в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җв”Җ ui_display      init display ILI9488 480Г—320 via SPI
  в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җв”Җ ui_touch        touch XPT2046 SPI
  в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җв”Җ ui_keypad       teclado analГіgico como LVGL indev
  в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җв”Җ ui_screens      gerenciamento carrossel (7 telas)
  в”Ӯ   в””в”Җв”Җ screens/        telas individuais (dashboard, devices, energy, ...)
  в””в”Җв”Җ include/       headers canГҙnicos compartilhados
      в”ңв”Җв”Җ pin_map.h           mapeamento GPIO
      в”ңв”Җв”Җ hardware_config.h   constantes de HW
      в”ңв”Җв”Җ alm_ids.h           enum ALM-001 a ALM-065
      в”ңв”Җв”Җ system_types.h      tipos base (system_state_t, safeoff_reason_t, ...)
      в”ңв”Җв”Җ global_state.h      struct do estado global
      в””в”Җв”Җ ...
```

## 3. SequГӘncia de Boot

```
app_main()
  в”Ӯ
  в”ңв”Җ init_nvs_safe()              recuperaГ§ГЈo de pГЎginas NVS
  в”ңв”Җ init_global_state()          g_gs = { SYSTEM_STATE_NORMAL, ... }
  в”ңв”Җ safety_controller_init()    safeoff_reason = NONE
  в”ңв”Җ alert_manager_init()        slots limpos
  в”ңв”Җ self_test_init()            prepara tabela de testes
  в”ңв”Җ hal_bus_init_all()          I2C(0), SPI(2), UART(PZEM)
  в”ңв”Җ circuit_breaker_init()      todos CLOSED
  в”ңв”Җ relay_init_safe()           todos relГ©s OFF
  в”ңв”Җ mcp3208_init() + acs712 + ad_keypad + pzem + ds18b20 + ds3231 + buzzer
  в”ңв”Җ cdn_energy_init()           acumuladores zerados
  в”ңв”Җ storage_sd_init()           monta FATFS SPI (falha nГЈo bloqueante)
  в”ңв”Җ thermal_fsm / ato_fsm / electric_fsm init
  в”ңв”Җ ui_display_init() + ui_screens_init()
  в”ңв”Җ api_rest_init()             servidor HTTP porta 80
  в”ңв”Җ wdt_advanced_init() + register(MAIN_LOOP, 2000ms)
  в””в”Җ self_test_run_all(10000ms)  testa HW, loga resultados
        вҶ“
   loop principal 50ms (while(1))
```

## 4. Loop Principal (50 ms)

Cada iteraГ§ГЈo executa na ordem:

```
1. circuit_breaker_update()        вҶ’ OPENвҶ’HALF_OPEN se timeout expirou
2. wdt_advanced_reset(MAIN_LOOP)   вҶ’ pet no WDT
3. read_temp()                     вҶ’ DS18B20 via circuit breaker
4. read_ato_level()                вҶ’ ADC via circuit breaker
5. thermal_fsm_update()            вҶ’ calcula estado tГ©rmico
6. ato_fsm_update()                вҶ’ calcula estado ATO
7. acs712_read_plug() Г— 10        вҶ’ correntes via circuit breaker
8. pzem_read_all()                 вҶ’ energia via circuit breaker
9. electric_fsm_update()           вҶ’ calcula estado elГ©trico
10. safety_controller_evaluate()   вҶ’ determina estado global
11. alert_manager_raise()          вҶ’ alarme se SAFE_OFF
12. relay_all_off() se SAFE_OFF/EMERGENCY
13. cdn_energy_update() Г— 10      вҶ’ acumula Wh
14. led_set()                      вҶ’ LED conforme estado
15. ui_screen_update_all() + lv_timer_handler()
16. vTaskDelay(50ms)
```

## 5. Safety Pipeline

```
Sensores вҶ’ FSMs вҶ’ Safety Controller вҶ’ Global State вҶ’ Relay Enforcement
   в”Ӯ          в”Ӯ            в”Ӯ                в”Ӯ               в”Ӯ
   в”Ӯ    thermal_fsm   force_emergency   SYSTEM_STATE_   relay_all_off()
   в”Ӯ    ato_fsm       force_safe_off    EMERGENCY       se >= SAFE_OFF
   в”Ӯ    electric_fsm   degraded         SAFE_OFF
   в”Ӯ                                    DEGRADED
   в”Ӯ                                    NORMAL
   в–ј
Circuit Breaker (por barramento)
   CLOSED вҶ’ falhas >= 5 вҶ’ OPEN вҶ’ 30s вҶ’ HALF_OPEN вҶ’ 3 sucessos вҶ’ CLOSED
```

**Prioridade**: `EMERGENCY > SAFE_OFF > DEGRADED > NORMAL`

Cada FSM publica flags `force_emergency`, `force_safe_off`, `degraded_condition`.
O Safety Controller usa a flag de maior prioridade como estado resultante.

## 6. Circuit Breaker

| Bus ID | Barramento | Threshold | Half-open | Monitorado por |
|--------|-----------|-----------|-----------|----------------|
| I2C | I2C-0 | 5 falhas | 30s | hal_bus (MCP23017, DS3231) |
| SPI_ADC | SPI2 MCP3208 | 5 | 30s | read_ato_level(), ACS712 reads |
| SPI_DISPLAY | SPI2 Display | 5 | 30s | UI LVGL |
| SPI_SD | SPI2 SD Card | 5 | 30s | storage_sd |
| UART_PZEM | UART PZEM | 5 | 30s | pzem_read_all() |
| DS18B20 | 1-Wire GPIO4 | 5 | 30s | read_temp() |

## 7. MГЎquinas de Estado

### Thermal FSM
```
        в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ
        в”Ӯ  NORMAL  в”Ӯ вҶҗ t dentro da faixa (sp Вұ h)
        в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”¬в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ
     t > sp+h в”Ӯ t < sp-h
        в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв–јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ
        в”Ӯ  ALERT   в”Ӯ вҶ’ request_cooler_on ou request_heater_on
        в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”¬в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ
  t >= critical в”Ӯ t >= extreme (se enabled)
        в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв–јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ        в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ
        в”Ӯ  CRITICAL    в”Ӯ        в”Ӯ EXTREME  в”Ӯ вҶ’ force_emergency
        в”Ӯ force_safe_offв”Ӯ        в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ
        в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ
        в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ
        в”Ӯ SENSOR_FAIL  в”Ӯ вҶҗ sample_valid == false
        в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ
```

### ATO FSM
```
        в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ
        в”Ӯ  NORMAL  в”Ӯ вҶҗ level вүҘ low
        в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”¬в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ
      level < low
        в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ
        в”Ӯ REFILLING в”Ӯ вҶ’ pump_request_on, timer countdown
        в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”¬в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ
  timeout 120s в”Ӯ   level вүҘ low
        в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв–јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ          в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ
        в”Ӯ  BLOCKED   в”Ӯ          в”Ӯ  NORMAL  в”Ӯ
        в”Ӯ pump OFF   в”Ӯ          в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ
        в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ
   level > overflow
        в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ
        в”Ӯ OVERFLOW в”Ӯ вҶ’ force_safe_off, blocked_latched
        в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ
        в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ
        в”Ӯ  ERROR   в”Ӯ вҶҗ sample_valid == false
        в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ
        в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ
        в”Ӯ DISABLED в”Ӯ вҶҗ cfg.enabled == false
        в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ
```

### Electric FSM
```
        в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ
        в”Ӯ  NORMAL  в”Ӯ вҶҗ potГӘncia total < limite - histerese
        в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”¬в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ
   potГӘncia na faixa de alerta
        в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ
        в”Ӯ HIGH_CONSUMPTION в”Ӯ вҶҗ entre (limite - h) e limite
        в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”¬в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ
  > limite total в”Ӯ > corrente por plug
        в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв–јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ
        в”Ӯ   OVERLOAD      в”Ӯ вҶ’ force_safe_off
        в”Ӯ (total ou plug) в”Ӯ
        в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ
        в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ
        в”ӮSENSOR_FAILв”Ӯ вҶҗ sample_valid == false
        в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ
```

## 8. Estados Globais

```
NORMAL    вҶ’ operaГ§ГЈo normal, todas as funГ§Гөes habilitadas
DEGRADED  вҶ’ falha nГЈo crГӯtica (ex: SD offline, display offline), operaГ§ГЈo continua
SAFE_OFF  вҶ’ condiГ§ГЈo de safety detectada, todos relГ©s desligados, monitora apenas
EMERGENCY вҶ’ temperatura extrema, emergГӘncia incondicional
```

TransiГ§Гөes: `NORMAL вҶ” DEGRADED`, `qualquer вҶ’ SAFE_OFF`, `qualquer вҶ’ EMERGENCY`
RecuperaГ§ГЈo de SAFE_OFF/EMERGENCY exige wizard ou reset.

## 9. Pilha Web API

```
httpd (esp_http_server porta 80)
  в””в”Җв”Җ auth_guard middleware
       в”ңв”Җв”Җ is_auth_path? вҶ’ libera /login e /logout
       в”ңв”Җв”Җ auth_middleware  вҶ’ valida X-Auth-Token (SHA-256 + RAM)
       в””в”Җв”Җ rate_limit_middleware вҶ’ 30 req/min/IP

Rotas:
  POST /api/v1/auth/login    вҶ’ {user, password} вҶ’ token (3600s)
  POST /api/v1/auth/logout   вҶ’ revoga token
  GET  /api/v1/status        вҶ’ estado global + alarmes
  GET  /api/v1/plugs         вҶ’ estado + corrente de cada plug
  POST /api/v1/plugs         вҶ’ {id, state} via safety pipeline
  GET  /api/v1/sensors       вҶ’ temperatura, ATO, keypad, RTC
  GET  /api/v1/energy        вҶ’ V, A, W, Wh, Hz, PF (PZEM)
  GET  /api/v1/alerts        вҶ’ alarmes ativos
  POST /api/v1/alerts        вҶ’ acknowledge todos alarmes
  GET  /api/v1/config        вҶ’ wizard_completed, monitor_only_mode
  POST /api/v1/config        вҶ’ altera configuraГ§ГЈo
  POST /api/v1/command       вҶ’ {cmd, plug_id, state} via command_validator
  GET  /api/v1/log           вҶ’ Гәltimos eventos
```

## 10. Pilha UI/HMI (LVGL v8.x)

```
lvgl (8.3)
  в”ңв”Җв”Җ display: ILI9488 480Г—320 via SPI (CS GPIO10, DC GPIO16, RST GPIO21, BL GPIO47)
  в”ңв”Җв”Җ touch:  XPT2046 SPI (CS, IRQ) вҶ’ LV_INDEV_TYPE_POINTER
  в”ңв”Җв”Җ keypad: AD Keypad via MCP3208 CH3 вҶ’ LV_INDEV_TYPE_KEYPAD
  в”ңв”Җв”Җ state_badge: lv_layer_top() com texto + cor (NORMALвң“/DEGRADEDвҡ /SAFE_OFFвӣ”/EMERGENCYрҹҡЁ)
  в””в”Җв”Җ carrossel 7 telas:
      0. Dashboard      вҶ’ temperatura, tomadas on, alarmes ativos, energia total
      1. Devices 1/2    вҶ’ P01-P05, P06-P10 (toggle ON/OFF + corrente)
      2. Energy         вҶ’ V, A, W, Wh, Hz, PF
      3. Alerts         вҶ’ lista scrollГЎvel + botГЈo ACK
      4. Menu           вҶ’ Config, Alarmes, Feed, ManutenГ§ГЈo, Wizard, Sobre
      5. Submenu        вҶ’ tensГЈo 127/220, temperatura alvo, potГӘncia mГЎxima
```

NavegaГ§ГЈo: touch/teclas avanГ§a/volta, timeout 60s volta ao Dashboard.

## 11. Armazenamento

| Dados | Local | Fatecimento |
|-------|-------|-------------|
| ConfiguraГ§ГЈo (wizard, modo) | NVS | RAM fallback |
| Alarmes ativos | RAM (`alert_slot_t[80]`) | Perde ao reset |
| Logs estruturados | SD FATFS (`/sdcard/{events,alerts,energy,audit}/log.txt`) | Opcional |
| Backup de config | SD FATFS (`/sdcard/config_backup.json`) | Opcional |
| Acumuladores CDN | RAM (`cdn_entry_t[10]`) | Inicia zerado |

## 12. Mapeamento de Pinos

| GPIO | FunГ§ГЈo | PerifГ©rico |
|------|--------|------------|
| 4 | DQ | DS18B20 (1-Wire) |
| 5 | OUT | RelГ© P01 |
| 6 | OUT | RelГ© P02 |
| 8 | SDA | I2C-0 |
| 9 | SCL | I2C-0 |
| 10 | CS | TFT |
| 11 | MOSI | SPI2 |
| 12 | MISO | SPI2 |
| 13 | SCK | SPI2 |
| 15 | CS | SD Card |
| 16 | DC | TFT |
| 17 | TX | PZEM UART |
| 18 | RX | PZEM UART |
| 21 | RST | TFT |
| 38 | CS | Touch XPT2046 |
| 39 | IRQ | Touch XPT2046 |
| 41 | CS | MCP3208 #1 (ACS712 P01-P08) |
| 42 | CS | MCP3208 #2 (P09, P10, ATO, Keypad) |
| 47 | BL | TFT Backlight |

**MCP23017 (I2C 0x20)**:
- GPA0-7 вҶ’ relГ©s P03-P10
- GPB2 вҶ’ LED Verde, GPB3 вҶ’ LED Amarelo, GPB4 вҶ’ LED Vermelho, GPB5 вҶ’ Buzzer

**MCP3208 #1 (CS=41)** CH0-7: ACS712 P01-P08
**MCP3208 #2 (CS=42)** CH0: P09, CH1: P10, CH2: ATO XKC-Y25-V, CH3: AD Keypad

## 13. EstratГ©gia de Watchdog

- `esp_task_wdt_init(10, true)`: WDT global 10s com panic
- `wdt_advanced` registra `main_loop` com reset a cada iteraГ§ГЈo (50ms)
- Em caso de hung > 10s, WDT forГ§a reset do SoC
- Tarefas UI e Web podem ser registradas no WDT individualmente

## 14. Mapa de Tarefas FreeRTOS

O firmware executa majoritariamente em uma Гәnica task (`app_main`), que implementa o loop principal de 50ms. O servidor HTTP cria tasks internas via `esp_http_server`.

| Task | FunГ§ГЈo | Prioridade | Stack | PerГӯodo | CriaГ§ГЈo |
|------|--------|------------|-------|---------|---------|
| `main` | Loop principal (leitura sensores + FSMs + UI) | 1 (configurable) | 8192 | 50ms | `app_main()` |
| `httpd` | Servidor HTTP (`esp_http_server`) | 5 (default) | 4096 | event-driven | `api_rest_init()` |
| `httpd_tx` | TransmissГЈo HTTP | 6 (default) | 4096 | event-driven | `esp_http_server` |
| `Tmr Svc` | FreeRTOS timer service | 1 | 2048 | 100ms tick | FreeRTOS |
| `esp_timer` | ESP32 high-res timer | 22 | 2048 | 1ms | `esp_timer` |
| `IDLE` | FreeRTOS idle + WDT | 0 | 1024 | вҖ” | FreeRTOS |

### PolГӯtica de Stack
- Task `main`: stack 8192 atual вҖ” se expandir funcionalidades, monitorar com `uxTaskGetStackHighWaterMark()`
- LVGL: renderizaГ§ГЈo ocorre na task `main` (sem task dedicada)
- SD card: opera via SPI na task `main` (sem task dedicada)

### WDT por Task
- `main`: resetado a cada iteraГ§ГЈo (timeout 2000ms)
- Demais tasks: retidas por `wdt_advanced_register()` conforme necessidade
- `IDLE`: WDT global 10s com panic

## 15. Novas Rotas API (v2)

Implementadas conforme PA-002:

```
POST /api/v1/auth/password вҶ’ define senha admin (primeiro uso)
GET  /api/v1/calibrate     вҶ’ valores atuais de calibraГ§ГЈo
POST /api/v1/feed          вҶ’ dispara Feed Mode
POST /api/v1/plugs/mode    вҶ’ define modo do plug (auto/manual/timer/delay/override)
GET  /api/v1/system        вҶ’ informaГ§Гөes de sistema (heap, versГЈo, uptime)
GET  /api/v1/wizard        вҶ’ status do wizard
POST /api/v1/wizard        вҶ’ completa wizard
```

## 16. Overlays de Estado (UI/HMI)

| Overlay | Estado | Cor de Fundo | AГ§ГЈo |
|---------|--------|-------------|------|
| SAFE_OFF | `SYSTEM_STATE_SAFE_OFF` | Vermelho escuro (80,0,0) | Mostra causa + restart status |
| EMERGENCY | `SYSTEM_STATE_EMERGENCY` | Vermelho intenso (120,0,0) | Mensagem de emergГӘncia |
| Wizard | `!wizard_completed` | Azul escuro (0,30,60) | InstruГ§Гөes de configuraГ§ГЈo |
| Alert | `critical_alerts_count > 0` | Preto (30,0,0) | Causa + aГ§ГЈo sugerida |
| MUTE | toggle key | Amarelo (255,200,0) | "[MUTE]" no canto superior direito |

## 17. Tratamento de Falhas

| Falha | AГ§ГЈo | RecuperaГ§ГЈo |
|-------|------|-------------|
| I2C MCP23017 sem resposta | Circuit breaker OPEN + alerta | HALF_OPEN apГіs 30s |
| SPI ADC sem resposta | Circuit breaker OPEN, ACS712/ATO indisponГӯveis | HALF_OPEN apГіs 30s |
| SD falha | Sistema continua sem storage | NГЈo recupera |
| PZEM sem resposta | Circuit breaker OPEN, energia nГЈo atualizada | HALF_OPEN apГіs 30s |
| DS18B20 sem resposta | Circuit breaker OPEN, temperatura default 25В°C | HALF_OPEN apГіs 30s |
| Temperatura crГӯtica | SAFE_OFF + alarme ALM-026 | Reset manual |
| NVS corrompido | NVS erase + recovery | AutomГЎtico |
| WDT timeout | Reset do SoC | POST + self-test |

===== FILE: C:\Users\6066180\OneDrive - Thomson Reuters Incorporated\Desktop\DDIno\firmware\concatena15.ps1 =====
param(
    [string]$RootPath = (Get-Location).Path
)

$ErrorActionPreference = "Stop"

Write-Host "Iniciando..."

$parts = 15

# Lista arquivos
$files = Get-ChildItem -Path $RootPath -File -Recurse | Sort-Object FullName
$total = $files.Count

Write-Host "Total arquivos: $total"

if ($total -eq 0) {
    Write-Host "Nenhum arquivo encontrado."
    exit
}

# Calcula quantidade por parte (SEM Math complexo)
$filesPerPart = $total / $parts

if ($filesPerPart -eq 0) {
    $filesPerPart = 1
}

# Remove arquivos antigos
for ($i = 1; $i -le $parts; $i++) {
    $name = "projeto_concatenado_part_{0:D2}_of_15.txt" -f $i
    if (Test-Path $name) {
        Remove-Item $name -Force
    }
}

# Loop principal
for ($part = 1; $part -le $parts; $part++) {

    $fileName = "projeto_concatenado_part_{0:D2}_of_15.txt" -f $part
    Write-Host "Gerando $fileName"

    $start = ($part - 1) * $filesPerPart
    $end = $start + $filesPerPart - 1

    if ($end -ge $total) {
        $end = $total - 1
    }

    Add-Content $fileName "***************************************INICIO DO ARQUIVO $part/15********************************"

    for ($i = $start; $i -le $end; $i++) {

        if ($i -ge $total) { break }

        $f = $files[$i]

        try {
            $content = Get-Content $f.FullName -Raw -ErrorAction Stop

            Add-Content $fileName ""
            Add-Content $fileName "===== FILE: $($f.FullName) ====="
            Add-Content $fileName $content
        }
        catch {
            Add-Content $fileName "ERRO AO LER: $($f.FullName)"
        }
    }

    Add-Content $fileName "***********************************FINAL DO ARQUIVO $part/15*************************"

    Write-Host "Parte $part concluida"
}

Write-Host "Finalizado."

===== FILE: C:\Users\6066180\OneDrive - Thomson Reuters Incorporated\Desktop\DDIno\firmware\core\circuit_breaker.c =====
// @requirement RNF-ELECTRICAL-001 Circuit breaker por barramento com fail count
// @requirement RF-ENERGY-008 ProteГ§ГЈo de sobrecorrente total via circuit breaker
#include "circuit_breaker.h"
#include "hardware_config.h"
#include "esp_timer.h"
#include <string.h>

static circuit_breaker_t s_breakers[CB_COUNT];

static const uint32_t DEFAULT_FAILURE_THRESHOLD = 5;
static const uint32_t DEFAULT_SUCCESS_THRESHOLD = 3;
static const uint32_t DEFAULT_HALF_OPEN_TIMEOUT_MS = 30000;
static const uint32_t DEFAULT_RECOVER_TIMEOUT_MS = 60000;

void circuit_breaker_init(void)
{
    memset(s_breakers, 0, sizeof(s_breakers));
    for (int i = 0; i < CB_COUNT; i++) {
        s_breakers[i].id = (cb_bus_id_t)i;
        s_breakers[i].state = CB_STATE_CLOSED;
        s_breakers[i].failure_threshold = DEFAULT_FAILURE_THRESHOLD;
        s_breakers[i].success_threshold = DEFAULT_SUCCESS_THRESHOLD;
        s_breakers[i].half_open_timeout_ms = DEFAULT_HALF_OPEN_TIMEOUT_MS;
        s_breakers[i].recover_timeout_ms = DEFAULT_RECOVER_TIMEOUT_MS;
    }
}

void circuit_breaker_record_success(cb_bus_id_t id)
{
    if (id >= CB_COUNT) return;
    circuit_breaker_t *cb = &s_breakers[id];
    cb->success_count++;
    cb->failure_count = 0;
    if (cb->state == CB_STATE_HALF_OPEN && cb->success_count >= cb->success_threshold) {
        cb->state = CB_STATE_CLOSED;
        cb->success_count = 0;
    }
}

void circuit_breaker_record_failure(cb_bus_id_t id)
{
    if (id >= CB_COUNT) return;
    circuit_breaker_t *cb = &s_breakers[id];
    cb->failure_count++;
    cb->last_failure_ms = esp_timer_get_time() / USEC_PER_MSEC;
    if (cb->state == CB_STATE_CLOSED && cb->failure_count >= cb->failure_threshold) {
        cb->state = CB_STATE_OPEN;
        cb->opened_at_ms = cb->last_failure_ms;
    } else if (cb->state == CB_STATE_HALF_OPEN) {
        cb->state = CB_STATE_OPEN;
        cb->opened_at_ms = cb->last_failure_ms;
    }
}

bool circuit_breaker_is_available(cb_bus_id_t id)
{
    if (id >= CB_COUNT) return false;
    circuit_breaker_t *cb = &s_breakers[id];
    if (cb->state == CB_STATE_CLOSED) return true;
    if (cb->state == CB_STATE_HALF_OPEN) return true;
    return false;
}

cb_state_t circuit_breaker_get_state(cb_bus_id_t id)
{
    if (id >= CB_COUNT) return CB_STATE_OPEN;
    return s_breakers[id].state;
}

void circuit_breaker_reset(cb_bus_id_t id)
{
    if (id >= CB_COUNT) return;
    circuit_breaker_t *cb = &s_breakers[id];
    cb->state = CB_STATE_CLOSED;
    cb->failure_count = 0;
    cb->success_count = 0;
    cb->opened_at_ms = 0;
}

void circuit_breaker_update(void)
{
    uint64_t now_ms = esp_timer_get_time() / USEC_PER_MSEC;
    for (int i = 0; i < CB_COUNT; i++) {
        circuit_breaker_t *cb = &s_breakers[i];
        if (cb->state == CB_STATE_OPEN) {
            if ((now_ms - cb->opened_at_ms) >= cb->half_open_timeout_ms) {
                cb->state = CB_STATE_HALF_OPEN;
                cb->success_count = 0;
            }
        }
    }
}

uint32_t circuit_breaker_open_count(cb_bus_id_t id)
{
    if (id >= CB_COUNT) return 0;
    return s_breakers[id].failure_count;
}


===== FILE: C:\Users\6066180\OneDrive - Thomson Reuters Incorporated\Desktop\DDIno\firmware\core\circuit_breaker.h =====
// @requirement RNF-ELECTRICAL-001 Circuit breaker pattern para barramentos
#ifndef FIRMWARE_CORE_CIRCUIT_BREAKER_H
#define FIRMWARE_CORE_CIRCUIT_BREAKER_H

#include <stdint.h>
#include <stdbool.h>
#include "esp_err.h"

typedef enum {
    CB_STATE_CLOSED,
    CB_STATE_OPEN,
    CB_STATE_HALF_OPEN
} cb_state_t;

typedef enum {
    CB_BUS_I2C,
    CB_BUS_SPI_ADC,
    CB_BUS_SPI_DISPLAY,
    CB_BUS_SPI_SD,
    CB_BUS_UART_PZEM,
    CB_BUS_DS18B20,
    CB_COUNT
} cb_bus_id_t;

typedef struct {
    cb_bus_id_t id;
    cb_state_t state;
    uint32_t failure_count;
    uint32_t success_count;
    uint64_t last_failure_ms;
    uint64_t opened_at_ms;
    uint32_t failure_threshold;
    uint32_t success_threshold;
    uint32_t half_open_timeout_ms;
    uint32_t recover_timeout_ms;
} circuit_breaker_t;

void circuit_breaker_init(void);
void circuit_breaker_record_success(cb_bus_id_t id);
void circuit_breaker_record_failure(cb_bus_id_t id);
bool circuit_breaker_is_available(cb_bus_id_t id);
cb_state_t circuit_breaker_get_state(cb_bus_id_t id);
void circuit_breaker_reset(cb_bus_id_t id);
void circuit_breaker_update(void);
uint32_t circuit_breaker_open_count(cb_bus_id_t id);

#endif


===== FILE: C:\Users\6066180\OneDrive - Thomson Reuters Incorporated\Desktop\DDIno\firmware\core\event_bus.c =====
// @requirement RF-GLOBAL-002 Barramento de eventos para comunicaзгo desacoplada
// @requirement RF-UI-INPUT-001 Eventos de UI e sistema roteados via event_bus
#include "event_bus.h"

#include <string.h>

#include "esp_log.h"

static const char *TAG = "event_bus";

typedef struct {
    event_id_t evt;
    event_callback_t cb;
    void *user_ctx;
    bool active;
} subscriber_t;

typedef struct {
    event_id_t evt;
    void *data;
} pending_event_t;

static subscriber_t s_subs[EVENT_BUS_MAX_SUBSCRIBERS];
static int s_sub_count;

static pending_event_t s_pending[EVENT_BUS_MAX_PENDING];
static int s_pending_head;
static int s_pending_tail;

esp_err_t event_bus_init(void)
{
    memset(s_subs, 0, sizeof(s_subs));
    s_sub_count = 0;
    s_pending_head = 0;
    s_pending_tail = 0;
    ESP_LOGI(TAG, "Event bus initialized");
    return ESP_OK;
}

esp_err_t event_bus_subscribe(event_id_t evt, event_callback_t cb, void *user_ctx)
{
    if (s_sub_count >= EVENT_BUS_MAX_SUBSCRIBERS) return ESP_ERR_NO_MEM;
    s_subs[s_sub_count].evt = evt;
    s_subs[s_sub_count].cb = cb;
    s_subs[s_sub_count].user_ctx = user_ctx;
    s_subs[s_sub_count].active = true;
    s_sub_count++;
    return ESP_OK;
}

esp_err_t event_bus_unsubscribe(event_id_t evt, event_callback_t cb)
{
    for (int i = 0; i < s_sub_count; i++) {
        if (s_subs[i].evt == evt && s_subs[i].cb == cb) {
            s_subs[i].active = false;
            return ESP_OK;
        }
    }
    return ESP_ERR_NOT_FOUND;
}

esp_err_t event_bus_publish(event_id_t evt, void *data)
{
    for (int i = 0; i < s_sub_count; i++) {
        if (s_subs[i].active && s_subs[i].evt == evt) {
            s_subs[i].cb(evt, data, s_subs[i].user_ctx);
        }
    }
    return ESP_OK;
}

esp_err_t event_bus_publish_isr(event_id_t evt, void *data)
{
    int next = (s_pending_head + 1) % EVENT_BUS_MAX_PENDING;
    if (next == s_pending_tail) return ESP_ERR_NO_MEM;
    s_pending[s_pending_head].evt = evt;
    s_pending[s_pending_head].data = data;
    s_pending_head = next;
    return ESP_OK;
}

void event_bus_process_pending(void)
{
    while (s_pending_tail != s_pending_head) {
        event_bus_publish(s_pending[s_pending_tail].evt, s_pending[s_pending_tail].data);
        s_pending_tail = (s_pending_tail + 1) % EVENT_BUS_MAX_PENDING;
    }
}



===== FILE: C:\Users\6066180\OneDrive - Thomson Reuters Incorporated\Desktop\DDIno\firmware\core\global_state.c =====
// @requirement RF-GLOBAL-001 Definiзгo de estados globais
// @requirement RF-GLOBAL-002 Transiзхes com prioridade e rastreabilidade
// @requirement RNF-GLOBAL-ANTIFLAP-001 Anti-flap em transiзхes
// @requirement RF-SAFEOFF-CAUSE-001 Rastreamento de causa SAFE_OFF
#include "global_state.h"

#include <stdio.h>
#include <string.h>

#include "esp_log.h"
#include "freertos/FreeRTOS.h"
#include "freertos/semphr.h"

#include "audit_log.h"
#include "config_manager.h"
#include "relay_abstraction.h"
#include "event_bus.h"
#include "hardware_config.h"

static const char *TAG = "global_state";

static global_state_t *s_gs = NULL;
static SemaphoreHandle_t s_mutex = NULL;

static uint64_t s_last_transition_ms;
static uint64_t s_flap_window_start_ms;
static uint32_t s_transition_count_in_window;

static void mutex_lock(void)
{
    if (s_mutex) {
        xSemaphoreTake(s_mutex, portMAX_DELAY);
    }
}

static void mutex_unlock(void)
{
    if (s_mutex) {
        xSemaphoreGive(s_mutex);
    }
}

static const char *state_to_str(system_state_t s)
{
    switch (s) {
        case SYSTEM_STATE_NORMAL:    return "NORMAL";
        case SYSTEM_STATE_DEGRADED:  return "DEGRADED";
        case SYSTEM_STATE_SAFE_OFF:  return "SAFE_OFF";
        case SYSTEM_STATE_EMERGENCY: return "EMERGENCY";
        default:                     return "UNKNOWN";
    }
}

static event_id_t state_to_event(system_state_t s)
{
    switch (s) {
        case SYSTEM_STATE_NORMAL:    return EVENT_ID_NORMAL;
        case SYSTEM_STATE_DEGRADED:  return EVENT_ID_DEGRADED;
        case SYSTEM_STATE_SAFE_OFF:  return EVENT_ID_SAFE_OFF;
        case SYSTEM_STATE_EMERGENCY: return EVENT_ID_EMERGENCY;
        default:                     return EVENT_ID_NONE;
    }
}

static bool check_antiflap(uint64_t now_ms)
{
    const antiflap_params_storage_t *cfg = config_get_antiflap();
    uint32_t cooldown_ms = cfg->cooldown_reentrada_s * MS_PER_SEC;
    uint32_t window_ms = cfg->janela_flap_s * MS_PER_SEC;
    uint32_t max_trans = cfg->max_transicoes_flap;

    if (s_last_transition_ms > 0 && (now_ms - s_last_transition_ms) < cooldown_ms) {
        return false;
    }
    if (s_flap_window_start_ms == 0 ||
        (now_ms - s_flap_window_start_ms) > window_ms) {
        s_flap_window_start_ms = now_ms;
        s_transition_count_in_window = 0;
    }
    s_transition_count_in_window++;
    return s_transition_count_in_window <= max_trans;
}

esp_err_t global_state_init(void)
{
    if (s_mutex == NULL) {
        s_mutex = xSemaphoreCreateMutex();
        if (!s_mutex) {
            return ESP_ERR_NO_MEM;
        }
    }
    s_last_transition_ms = 0;
    s_flap_window_start_ms = 0;
    s_transition_count_in_window = 0;
    return ESP_OK;
}

void global_state_bind(global_state_t *gs)
{
    s_gs = gs;
    (void)global_state_init();
}

esp_err_t global_state_get_snapshot(global_state_t *out)
{
    if (!out || !s_gs) {
        return ESP_ERR_INVALID_ARG;
    }
    mutex_lock();
    memcpy(out, s_gs, sizeof(*out));
    mutex_unlock();
    return ESP_OK;
}

const global_state_t *global_state_get_snapshot_ptr(void)
{
    return s_gs;
}

global_state_t *global_state_get_write_ptr(void)
{
    return s_gs;
}

esp_err_t global_state_set_health_flag(global_state_health_field_t field, bool ok)
{
    if (!s_gs) {
        return ESP_ERR_INVALID_STATE;
    }
    mutex_lock();
    switch (field) {
        case GS_HEALTH_TEMP:      s_gs->temp_ok = ok; break;
        case GS_HEALTH_ATO:      s_gs->ato_ok = ok; break;
        case GS_HEALTH_PZEM:      s_gs->pzem_ok = ok; break;
        case GS_HEALTH_SD:        s_gs->sd_ok = ok; break;
        case GS_HEALTH_WIFI:      s_gs->wifi_ok = ok; break;
        case GS_HEALTH_UI:        s_gs->ui_ok = ok; break;
        case GS_HEALTH_ELECTRIC:  s_gs->electric_ok = ok; break;
        case GS_HEALTH_SELFTEST:  s_gs->selftest_passed = ok; break;
        default:
            mutex_unlock();
            return ESP_ERR_INVALID_ARG;
    }
    mutex_unlock();
    return ESP_OK;
}

esp_err_t global_state_transition(system_state_t next_state, safeoff_reason_t reason,
                                   const char *source_alm, const char *source_module,
                                   uint64_t now_s)
{
    if (!s_gs) {
        return ESP_ERR_INVALID_STATE;
    }

    uint64_t now_ms = now_s * MS_PER_SEC;

    mutex_lock();
    system_state_t prev = s_gs->system_state;

    if (prev == next_state && s_gs->safeoff_reason == reason) {
        mutex_unlock();
        return ESP_OK;
    }

    /* @requirement RF-GLOBAL-002 EMERGENCY nгo rebaixa automaticamente. */
    if (prev == SYSTEM_STATE_EMERGENCY && next_state != SYSTEM_STATE_EMERGENCY) {
        ESP_LOGW(TAG, "Transicao EMERGENCY->%s bloqueada (saida controlada apenas)",
                 state_to_str(next_state));
        mutex_unlock();
        return ESP_ERR_INVALID_STATE;
    }

    /* @requirement RF-GLOBAL-SAFEOFF-EXIT-001 SAFE_OFF nгo retorna a NORMAL/DEGRADED
     * automaticamente; apenas escalonamento para EMERGENCY й permitido. */
    if (prev == SYSTEM_STATE_SAFE_OFF &&
        next_state != SYSTEM_STATE_SAFE_OFF &&
        next_state != SYSTEM_STATE_EMERGENCY) {
        ESP_LOGW(TAG, "Transicao SAFE_OFF->%s bloqueada (exige saida controlada)",
                 state_to_str(next_state));
        mutex_unlock();
        return ESP_ERR_INVALID_STATE;
    }

    /* Anti-flap aplica-se apenas a transiзхes de recuperaзгo/rebaixamento
     * (NORMAL/DEGRADED). Escalonamento de seguranзa nunca й bloqueado. */
    if ((next_state == SYSTEM_STATE_NORMAL || next_state == SYSTEM_STATE_DEGRADED) &&
        !check_antiflap(now_ms)) {
        ESP_LOGW(TAG, "ANTIFLAP bloqueou %s->%s", state_to_str(prev), state_to_str(next_state));
        mutex_unlock();
        return ESP_ERR_INVALID_STATE;
    }

    s_gs->system_state = next_state;

    if (next_state == SYSTEM_STATE_SAFE_OFF) {
        s_gs->safeoff_reason = reason;
        snprintf(s_gs->safeoff_entered_at, sizeof(s_gs->safeoff_entered_at),
                 "%llu", (unsigned long long)now_s);
        if (source_alm) {
            snprintf(s_gs->safeoff_source_alm, sizeof(s_gs->safeoff_source_alm),
                     "%s", source_alm);
        } else {
            s_gs->safeoff_source_alm[0] = '\0';
        }
        s_gs->electric_ok = false;
        relay_abstraction_all_off();
    } else if (next_state == SYSTEM_STATE_EMERGENCY) {
        s_gs->electric_ok = false;
        relay_abstraction_all_off();
    } else if (next_state == SYSTEM_STATE_NORMAL) {
        s_gs->safeoff_reason = SAFEOFF_REASON_NONE;
        s_gs->safeoff_source_alm[0] = '\0';
        s_gs->safeoff_entered_at[0] = '\0';
        s_gs->electric_ok = true;
    } else if (next_state == SYSTEM_STATE_DEGRADED) {
        if (prev == SYSTEM_STATE_SAFE_OFF || prev == SYSTEM_STATE_EMERGENCY) {
            s_gs->safeoff_reason = SAFEOFF_REASON_NONE;
            s_gs->safeoff_source_alm[0] = '\0';
        }
    }

    s_last_transition_ms = now_ms;
    mutex_unlock();

    audit_log_state_change(state_to_str(prev), state_to_str(next_state),
                           source_module ? source_module : "global_state_transition");
    event_bus_publish(state_to_event(next_state), NULL);

    ESP_LOGW(TAG, "GLOBAL_TRANSITION prev=%s next=%s reason=%d alm=%s module=%s ts=%llu",
             state_to_str(prev), state_to_str(next_state), (int)reason,
             source_alm ? source_alm : "-",
             source_module ? source_module : "-",
             (unsigned long long)now_s);

    return ESP_OK;
}



===== FILE: C:\Users\6066180\OneDrive - Thomson Reuters Incorporated\Desktop\DDIno\firmware\core\safety_controller.c =====
// @requirement RF-GLOBAL-001 Definiзгo de estados globais
// @requirement RF-GLOBAL-002 Transiзхes de estado global com anti-flap
// @requirement RF-GLOBAL-003 Sinais sonoros/visuais em estado crнtico
// @requirement RF-GLOBAL-004 Rastreamento de causa de SAFE_OFF
// @requirement RF-GLOBAL-SAFEOFF-EXIT-001 Prй-condiзхes saнda de SAFE_OFF
// @requirement RF-GLOBAL-EMERG-EXIT-001 Saнda controlada de EMERGENCY
// @requirement RNF-GLOBAL-ANTIFLAP-001 Estabilizaзгo de retorno
#include "safety_controller.h"

#include <stdio.h>
#include <string.h>

#include "esp_log.h"

#include "audit_log.h"
#include "relay_abstraction.h"
#include "event_log.h"
#include "hardware_config.h"

static const char *TAG = "safety_controller";

static safety_context_t s_ctx;

void safety_controller_init(global_state_t *gs)
{
    if (!gs) return;
    memset(&s_ctx, 0, sizeof(s_ctx));
    gs->safeoff_reason = SAFEOFF_REASON_NONE;
    gs->safeoff_entered_at[0] = '\0';
    gs->safeoff_source_alm[0] = '\0';
    gs->electric_ok = true;
}

esp_err_t global_state_enter_safeoff(global_state_t *gs, safeoff_reason_t reason,
                                      const char *source_alm, const char *source_module,
                                      uint64_t now_s)
{
    if (!gs) return ESP_ERR_INVALID_ARG;
    if (reason == SAFEOFF_REASON_NONE) return ESP_ERR_INVALID_ARG;
    if (gs->system_state == SYSTEM_STATE_SAFE_OFF) return ESP_OK;

    system_state_t prev = gs->system_state;
    gs->system_state = SYSTEM_STATE_SAFE_OFF;
    gs->safeoff_reason = reason;
    snprintf(gs->safeoff_entered_at, sizeof(gs->safeoff_entered_at), "%llu",
             (unsigned long long)now_s);
    if (source_alm) {
        snprintf(gs->safeoff_source_alm, sizeof(gs->safeoff_source_alm), "%s", source_alm);
    } else {
        gs->safeoff_source_alm[0] = '\0';
    }
    gs->electric_ok = false;
    relay_abstraction_all_off();

    ESP_LOGE("safety", "SAFE_OFF entered from %d reason=%d alm=%s module=%s",
             (int)prev, (int)reason, source_alm ? source_alm : "?", source_module ? source_module : "?");
    audit_log_state_change(system_state_to_str(prev), "SAFE_OFF", source_module ? source_module : "enter_safeoff");
    return ESP_OK;
}

esp_err_t global_state_enter_emergency(global_state_t *gs, const char *source_module, uint64_t now_s)
{
    if (!gs) return ESP_ERR_INVALID_ARG;
    if (gs->system_state >= SYSTEM_STATE_EMERGENCY) return ESP_OK;

    system_state_t prev = gs->system_state;
    gs->system_state = SYSTEM_STATE_EMERGENCY;
    gs->electric_ok = false;
    relay_abstraction_all_off();

    ESP_LOGE("safety", "EMERGENCY entered from %d module=%s", (int)prev, source_module ? source_module : "?");
    audit_log_state_change(system_state_to_str(prev), "EMERGENCY", source_module ? source_module : "enter_emergency");
    return ESP_OK;
}

esp_err_t global_state_enter_degraded(global_state_t *gs, const char *source_module)
{
    if (!gs) return ESP_ERR_INVALID_ARG;
    if (gs->system_state >= SYSTEM_STATE_DEGRADED) return ESP_OK;

    system_state_t prev = gs->system_state;
    gs->system_state = SYSTEM_STATE_DEGRADED;
    ESP_LOGW("safety", "DEGRADED entered module=%s", source_module ? source_module : "?");
    audit_log_state_change(system_state_to_str(prev), "DEGRADED", source_module ? source_module : "enter_degraded");
    return ESP_OK;
}

static bool check_antiflap(system_state_t next, uint64_t now_ms)
{
    (void)next;
    if (s_ctx.last_transition_ms == 0) return true;
    uint64_t elapsed = now_ms - s_ctx.last_transition_ms;
    if (elapsed < HW_ANTIFLAP_COOLDOWN_MS) return false;

    if (s_ctx.flap_window_start_ms == 0) {
        s_ctx.flap_window_start_ms = now_ms;
        s_ctx.transition_count_in_window = 0;
    }
    if ((now_ms - s_ctx.flap_window_start_ms) > HW_ANTIFLAP_WINDOW_MS) {
        s_ctx.flap_window_start_ms = now_ms;
        s_ctx.transition_count_in_window = 0;
    }
    s_ctx.transition_count_in_window++;
    if (s_ctx.transition_count_in_window > HW_ANTIFLAP_MAX_TRANSITIONS) return false;
    return true;
}

void safety_controller_evaluate(global_state_t *gs, const safety_inputs_t *in, uint64_t now_s)
{
    if (!gs || !in) return;

    /* @requirement RF-GLOBAL-002 Prioridade EMERGENCY > SAFE_OFF > DEGRADED > NORMAL.
     * Esta funзгo muta o gs recebido (contrato testбvel) e replica os efeitos
     * centrais: relay_abstraction_all_off em SAFE_OFF/EMERGENCY e audit trail.
     * Saнda de SAFE_OFF/EMERGENCY nunca й automбtica (ver can_exit_*). */
    const system_state_t prev = gs->system_state;
    system_state_t next;

    if (in->emergency_condition) {
        next = SYSTEM_STATE_EMERGENCY;
    } else if (in->safeoff_condition) {
        next = SYSTEM_STATE_SAFE_OFF;
    } else if (in->degraded_condition || !in->all_sensors_valid || !in->selftest_passed) {
        /* Nгo rebaixar SAFE_OFF/EMERGENCY para DEGRADED automaticamente. */
        if (prev == SYSTEM_STATE_SAFE_OFF || prev == SYSTEM_STATE_EMERGENCY) return;
        next = SYSTEM_STATE_DEGRADED;
    } else {
        /* @requirement RF-GLOBAL-SAFEOFF-EXIT-001 / RF-GLOBAL-EMERG-EXIT-001
         * Retorno a NORMAL somente a partir de NORMAL/DEGRADED. */
        if (prev != SYSTEM_STATE_NORMAL && prev != SYSTEM_STATE_DEGRADED) return;
        next = SYSTEM_STATE_NORMAL;
    }

    if (next == prev) return;

    /* EMERGENCY nгo rebaixa automaticamente. */
    if (prev == SYSTEM_STATE_EMERGENCY && next != SYSTEM_STATE_EMERGENCY) return;

    if (!check_antiflap(next, now_s * MS_PER_SEC)) {
        ESP_LOGW(TAG, "ANTIFLAP: transicao %s->%s bloqueada (max %d em %dms)",
                 system_state_to_str(prev), system_state_to_str(next),
                 HW_ANTIFLAP_MAX_TRANSITIONS, HW_ANTIFLAP_WINDOW_MS);
        return;
    }

    if (next == SYSTEM_STATE_SAFE_OFF) {
        gs->safeoff_reason = in->safeoff_reason_if_any;
        snprintf(gs->safeoff_entered_at, sizeof(gs->safeoff_entered_at), "%llu",
                 (unsigned long long)now_s);
        if (in->safeoff_source_alm) {
            snprintf(gs->safeoff_source_alm, sizeof(gs->safeoff_source_alm), "%s", in->safeoff_source_alm);
        } else {
            gs->safeoff_source_alm[0] = '\0';
        }
        gs->electric_ok = false;
    } else if (next == SYSTEM_STATE_EMERGENCY) {
        gs->electric_ok = false;
    } else if (next == SYSTEM_STATE_NORMAL) {
        gs->safeoff_reason = SAFEOFF_REASON_NONE;
        gs->safeoff_source_alm[0] = '\0';
        gs->electric_ok = true;
    } else if (next == SYSTEM_STATE_DEGRADED) {
        if (prev == SYSTEM_STATE_SAFE_OFF || prev == SYSTEM_STATE_EMERGENCY) {
            gs->safeoff_reason = SAFEOFF_REASON_NONE;
            gs->safeoff_source_alm[0] = '\0';
        }
    }

    gs->system_state = next;
    s_ctx.last_transition_ms = now_s * MS_PER_SEC;

    if (next == SYSTEM_STATE_SAFE_OFF || next == SYSTEM_STATE_EMERGENCY) {
        relay_abstraction_all_off();
    }

    audit_log_state_change(system_state_to_str(prev), system_state_to_str(next),
                           in->transition_cause ? in->transition_cause : "safety_controller");

    ESP_LOGW(TAG, "GLOBAL_TRANSITION prev=%s next=%s cause=%s",
             system_state_to_str(prev), system_state_to_str(next),
             in->transition_cause ? in->transition_cause : "N/A");
}

bool safety_controller_can_exit_safeoff(const global_state_t *gs, const safety_inputs_t *in, uint64_t now_s)
{
    if (gs->system_state != SYSTEM_STATE_SAFE_OFF) return false;
    if (!in) return false;
    if (in->emergency_condition) return false;
    if (!in->safeoff_cause_resolved) return false;
    if (!in->all_sensors_valid) return false;
    if (!in->selftest_passed) return false;
    if (!in->manual_ack_received) return false;

    if (in->cause_resolved_at_ms > 0) {
        uint64_t elapsed = (now_s * MS_PER_SEC) - in->cause_resolved_at_ms;
        if (elapsed < (HW_SAFEOFF_CAUSE_STABLE_S * MS_PER_SEC)) return false;
    }

    return true;
}

bool safety_controller_can_exit_emergency(const global_state_t *gs, const safety_inputs_t *in, uint64_t now_s)
{
    if (gs->system_state != SYSTEM_STATE_EMERGENCY) return false;
    if (!in) return false;
    if (!in->emergency_resolved) return false;
    if (!in->all_sensors_valid) return false;
    if (!in->manual_ack_received) return false;

    if (in->cause_resolved_at_ms > 0) {
        uint64_t elapsed = (now_s * MS_PER_SEC) - in->cause_resolved_at_ms;
        if (elapsed < (HW_EMERGENCY_CAUSE_STABLE_S * MS_PER_SEC)) return false;
    }

    return true;
}

// @requirement RF-GLOBAL-001 a RF-GLOBAL-004 Estados globais e transiГ§Гөes
// @requirement RF-GLOBAL-SAFEOFF-EXIT-001 SaГӯda segura de SAFE_OFF
// @requirement RF-GLOBAL-EMERG-EXIT-001 SaГӯda controlada de EMERGENCY
#ifndef FIRMWARE_CORE_SAFETY_CONTROLLER_H
#define FIRMWARE_CORE_SAFETY_CONTROLLER_H

#include <stdint.h>
#include <stdbool.h>
#include "esp_err.h"
#include "system_types.h"
#include "global_state.h"

typedef struct {
    bool emergency_condition;
    bool safeoff_condition;
    bool degraded_condition;
    safeoff_reason_t safeoff_reason_if_any;
    const char *safeoff_source_alm;
    const char *transition_cause;
    bool all_sensors_valid;
    bool selftest_passed;
    bool emergency_resolved;
    bool safeoff_cause_resolved;
    bool manual_ack_received;
    uint64_t cause_resolved_at_ms;
} safety_inputs_t;

typedef struct {
    uint64_t last_transition_ms;
    uint64_t flap_window_start_ms;
    uint32_t transition_count_in_window;
    uint64_t last_safeoff_exit_attempt_ms;
    uint32_t safeoff_stabilization_count;
} safety_context_t;

void safety_controller_init(global_state_t *gs);
void safety_controller_evaluate(global_state_t *gs, const safety_inputs_t *in, uint64_t now_s);
bool safety_controller_can_exit_safeoff(const global_state_t *gs, const safety_inputs_t *in, uint64_t now_s);
bool safety_controller_can_exit_emergency(const global_state_t *gs, const safety_inputs_t *in, uint64_t now_s);

esp_err_t global_state_enter_safeoff(global_state_t *gs, safeoff_reason_t reason,
                                     const char *source_alm, const char *source_module,
                                     uint64_t now_s);
esp_err_t global_state_enter_emergency(global_state_t *gs, const char *source_module, uint64_t now_s);
esp_err_t global_state_enter_degraded(global_state_t *gs, const char *source_module);

/* @requirement RF-AUDIT RF-GLOBAL-002 mapeamento estadoвҶ’string */
static inline const char *system_state_to_str(system_state_t s)
{
    switch (s) {
        case SYSTEM_STATE_NORMAL:    return "NORMAL";
        case SYSTEM_STATE_DEGRADED:  return "DEGRADED";
        case SYSTEM_STATE_SAFE_OFF:  return "SAFE_OFF";
        case SYSTEM_STATE_EMERGENCY: return "EMERGENCY";
        default:                     return "UNKNOWN";
    }
}

#endif

# ADC_CONDITIONING_SPEC

| Requisito | RF-HW-ADC-* / AF.3 |
|-----------|-------------------|

## MCP3208 (SPI)

| Canal | FunГ§ГЈo | CS |
|-------|--------|-----|
| #1 | ACS712 P01вҖ“P05 (condicionado) | GPIO41 |
| #2 CH2 | ATO digital ON/OFF | GPIO42 |

- Clock SPI: 1 MHz (`HW_SPI_CLK_MCP3208_HZ`)
- Faixa contagem: 0вҖ“4095 (`HW_ADC_MAX_COUNT`)
- Vref lГіgica: 3.3 V (`HW_ADC_VREF_MV`)

## ATO digital (RF-ATO-DIGITAL-001)

- Entrada condicionada 0вҖ“3.3 V
- LOW/HIGH/overflow configurГЎveis via Wizard (`low_level_adc`, `high_level_adc`, `overflow_margin_adc`)
- Debounce: 3 amostras (`ato_fsm.c`)

## ACS712 20A (RF-PLUG-003)

- AlimentaГ§ГЈo sensor: 5 V (`HW_ACS712_SUPPLY_MV`)
- SaГӯda condicionada para 0вҖ“3.3 V (`HW_ACS712_CONDITIONED_TO_3V3`)
- Offset/gain calibrГЎvel por canal NVS
- RMS obrigatГіrio (`driver_acs712.c`)

## Keypad AD (RF-UI-INPUT-*)

- AlimentaГ§ГЈo 5 V, entrada condicionada ADC (`HW_AD_KEYPAD_ADC_CONDITIONED`)

ImplementaГ§ГЈo: `drivers/driver_mcp3208.c`, `drivers/driver_acs712.c`, `drivers/driver_ad_keypad.c`


===== FILE: C:\Users\6066180\OneDrive - Thomson Reuters Incorporated\Desktop\DDIno\firmware\docs\adr\ADR_OTA_DEFERRED.md =====
# ADR-OTA-DEFERRED: OTA via Application Firmware Deferida

## Status
ACCEPTED (2026-06-28)

## Context
O SRS v3.11 (RF-HW-OTA-001) especifica suporte a OTA (Over-The-Air) para atualizacao de firmware. No entanto, a implementacao de OTA confiavel dentro da aplicacao apresenta riscos:

1. **Complexidade de rollback**: Gerenciar fallback por software em caso de falha de boot apos OTA.
2. **Uso de flash**: Particao OTA consome flash que pode ser melhor utilizado para storage (NVS / SPIFFS).
3. **Seguranca**: Validacao de imagem OTA e protecao contra brick requer assinatura e verificacao robusta.
4. **Integracao com bootloader**: O ESP-IDF oferece suporte nativo a OTA via `esp_https_ota`, mas a integracao segura requer servidor dedicado e certificados.

## Decision
OTA via application firmware foi **DEFERIDA** para uma versao futura (v2.0.0). A versao atual (F1.0.0) nao implementa OTA. Atualizacoes de firmware serao feitas via:

- **USB/UART**: Atraves do bootloader do ESP32-S3 (`esptool.py` / `idf.py flash`).
- **Conexao serial dedicada**: Pino de boot (GPIO0) acessivel no conector de programacao.

## Consequences

### Positive
- Reducao do risco de brick durante atualizacao remota.
- Mais flash disponivel para armazenamento local (NVS + SPIFFS).
- Menos codigo na aplicacao para gerenciamento de particoes OTA.

### Negative
- Atualizacoes requerem acesso fisico ao dispositivo ou conexao serial.
- Nao e possivel corrigir bugs de firmware remotamente.
- Requer planejamento para implementacao futura com servidor OTA dedicado e assinatura de imagem.

## Compliance Note
O requisito RF-HW-OTA-001 esta marcado como **DEFERRED** no RTM. A implementacao sera reavaliada na proxima revisao major (v2.0.0).

# Adendos Funcionais e Blocos Normativos

## AF.1 вҖ” CorreГ§ГЈo de pinagem do display
Conforme SRS TГ©cnico Consolidado, o barramento SPI ILI9488 opera em modo 4-wire com CS dedicado (GPIO10) e DC via GPIO11.

## AF.2 вҖ” ExpansГЈo de ALM para sensores
Adicionados ALM-060 a ALM-065 para falhas de sensor ACS712 e PZEM.

## Blocos Normativos
- BLOCO 01/N: Prioridade heater > cooler: HEATER e COOLER nunca simultГўneos.
- BLOCO 02/N: Lockout mГӯnimo 500ms entre OFFвҶ’ON.
- BLOCO 03/N: SAFE_OFF exige causa resolvida + ACK.
- BLOCO 04/N: EMERGENCY sinaliza buzzer + LED atГ© power cycle.
- BLOCO 05/N: Wizard ao primeiro boot obrigatГіrio.
- BLOCO 06/N: Log persistente em SD com rotaГ§ГЈo.
- BLOCO 07/N: OTA com rollback.
- BLOCO 08/N: Mutex SPI para barramento compartilhado.
- BLOCO 09/N: NVS com schema versionado.
- BLOCO 10/N: Self-test obrigatГіrio no boot.
- BLOCO 11/N: Factory reset via hardware.
- BLOCO 12/N: API REST com JWT.
- BLOCO 13/N: Web dashboard SPA.

| 1 | ERR_AUTH_INVALID | 401 | Credencial invГЎlida | Login falhou |
| 2 | ERR_AUTH_FORBIDDEN | 403 | Sem permissГЈo | Role insuficiente |
| 3 | ERR_STATE_NOT_ALLOWED | 409 | Estado nГЈo permite aГ§ГЈo | SAFE_OFF/EMERGENCY |

| 5 | ERR_VALIDATION_ERROR | 400 | ParГўmetro invГЎlido | command_validator |

# Audit Scope вҖ” Monitor AquГЎrio Inteligente

## Version

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|

| Date | 2026-06-27 |
| Firmware Version | compliance-fix-v1 |

## Scope Boundaries

### In Scope

The following directories and file types are included in compliance audit:

| Directory | Includes | Excludes |
|-----------|----------|----------|
| `main/` | All `.c`, `.h`, `CMakeLists.txt`, `idf_component.yml` | вҖ” |
| `core/` | All `.c`, `.h` | вҖ” |
| `drivers/` | All `.c`, `.h` | вҖ” |
| `services/` | All `.c`, `.h` | вҖ” |
| `fsm/` | All `.c`, `.h` | вҖ” |
| `hal/` | All `.c`, `.h` | вҖ” |
| `web/` | All `.c`, `.h` | вҖ” |
| `ui/` | All `.c`, `.h` | вҖ” |
| `security/` | All `.c`, `.h` | вҖ” |
| `include/` | All `.h` | вҖ” |
| `test/` | All `.c`, `CMakeLists.txt` | вҖ” |
| `docs/` | All `.md` | вҖ” |
| `scripts/` | All files | вҖ” |
| Root config files | `partitions.csv`, `sdkconfig.defaults`, `CMakeLists.txt` | вҖ” |

### Out of Scope

| Path | Reason |
|------|--------|
| `managed_components/` | Third-party vendor code (LVGL, ESP-IDF managed) вҖ” not subject to project audit; version/pinned reference recorded in THIRD_PARTY_COMPONENTS.md |
| `build/` | Build artifacts вҖ” regenerated |
| `test/` (test frameworks) | Test harness code is in scope; test runner infrastructure (Unity, CMock) is third-party |
| `concatena.ps1` (root) | Developer utility script вҖ” not part of firmware deliverable |
| Any `*.bin`, `*.elf`, `*.map`, `*.o` | Build artifacts |
| Any `*.pyc`, `__pycache__/` | Python cache |
| IDE/editor files (`.vscode/`, `.idea/`, `*.swp`) | Developer environment |

## Audit Criteria

### Mandatory Requirements (P0) вҖ” Blocking

| Criterion | Description |
|-----------|-------------|
| BUILD | `idf.py build` completes with zero errors, zero warnings (`-Wall -Wextra -Werror`) |
| SAFE_OFF | All 10 rules: relay_all_off, reason/timestamp/source ALM, audit log, API state, UI overlay, command blocking, diagnostic preservation |
| EMERGENCY | Latching with reason, relay_all_off, manual reset only |
| GLOBAL_STATE | Thread-safe transitions with priority validation (EMERGENCY > SAFE_OFF > DEGRADED > NORMAL) |
| COMMAND_VALIDATOR | All write paths gated by `can_*` checks |
| NO_BYPASS | UI/API never calls `relay_set()`, `gpio_set_level()`, `mcp23017_write_gpio()` directly |
| ZERO_HARDCODE | All operational values via ConfigRoot / param_catalog.h |
| AUTH | No hardcoded credentials; SHA-256 hashed password in NVS; session tokens in RAM |
| STORAGE_ATOMIC | Critical writes use `.tmp` + fsync + rename; RAM fallback when SD absent |

### Recommended Requirements (P1) вҖ” Non-blocking

| Criterion | Description |
|-----------|-------------|
| FREE RTOS TASKS | Dedicated tasks with priorities (not single-loop) |
| UNIT TESTS | `idf.py test` passes for all test/ components |
| RTM_COVERAGE | 100% of SRS requirements mapped in RTM.md |
| COMPLIANCE_REPORT | SRS_COMPLIANCE_IMPLEMENTATION_REPORT.md with evidence for every requirement |
| WDT_COVERAGE | Task watchdog or advanced WDT for all critical paths |

### Out of Scope Requirements

| Requirement | Status | Reason |
|-------------|--------|--------|
| RF-OTA-001..005 | Deferred | Post-compliance epic |
| RF-EMAIL-001 (SMTP) | Deferred | Future epic |
| RF-PH-001 (pH sensor) | Deferred | Future epic |
| RF-SENSOR-REDUNDANCY-001 | Deferred | Future epic |

# RelatГіrio Final de Compliance вҖ” DDIno

## 1. Resumo Executivo

| Campo | Valor |

## 4. CorreГ§Гөes por Bloco

### P0-001 вҖ” ConfigRoot canГҙnico
JГЎ existente e funcional: `config_root_t` em `config_root.h` utiliza structs canГҙnicas de `param_catalog.h` (thermal_params_storage_t, ato_params_storage_t, etc.) com CRC32, schema version, commit e rollback. Os tipos sugeridos pelo prompt (config_thermal_t, etc.) tГӘm campos diferentes dos definidos na SRS; prevalece a SRS.

### P0-002 вҖ” Safety Gate (NOVO)
Criado `services/safety_gate.c/h` com `safety_gate_can_enable_automation()`:
- Verifica wizard_completed
- Verifica monitor_only_mode
- Verifica SAFE_OFF / EMERGENCY
- Verifica selftest_passed
- Verifica hw_ok

### P0-003 вҖ” Command Dispatcher (NOVO)
Criado `services/command_dispatcher.c/h` com `command_dispatch_execute()`:
- Rota comandos via safety_gate + command_validator
- Helpers: toggle_plug, ack_alert, start_feed, set_mode

### P0-004 вҖ” SAFE_OFF Record (NOVO)
Criado `services/safeoff_record.c/h`:
- safeoff_record_entry_t com reason, source_alm, timestamps, duraГ§ГЈo
- safeoff_record_t ring de 16 entradas
- PersistГӘncia em NVS via storage_manager
- safeoff_record_append() / safeoff_record_resolve_latest()

### P0-005 вҖ” FreeRTOS Tasks
JГЎ existente: 7 tasks definidas em app_main.c conforme task_manager.h (safety_core, sensors, plug_control, storage, ui, web, diag) com prioridades, stacks, cores, WDT timeouts e heartbeat.

### P0-006 вҖ” Storage AtГҙmico + Ring Buffer (NOVO)
Criado `services/storage_atomic.c/h` com ring buffer circular de 256 entradas, thread-safe, para logs em RAM quando SD indisponГӯvel.

### P1-001 вҖ” Log Manager (NOVO)
Criado `services/log_manager.c/h` + atualizado `ui_screen_logs.c`:
- log_record_t com severity, timestamp, module, message

### P1-004 вҖ” API REST
JГЎ existente e completa: api_rest.c com 27 handlers, api_auth.c com SHA-256 + token bearer, api_rate_limit.c com rate limiting por IP.

### P1-005 вҖ” Health Matrix
JГЎ existente e completa: health_matrix.c com 14 subsistemas, 6 estados (OK/DEGRADED/FAILED/OPEN/HALF_OPEN/CLOSED), funГ§ГЈo aggregate.

# CorreГ§ГЈo de Compliance SRS вҖ” RelatГіrio Final

- Compliance alvo: >= 95%

- Build executado: NГғO вҖ” ESP-IDF (`idf.py`) nГЈo estГЎ instalado nesta mГЎquina.
- Resultado do build: PENDENTE вҖ” DADO NГғO FORNECIDO NO DOCUMENTO FONTE (ambiente sem toolchain)
- Testes executados: NГғO automatizados nesta mГЎquina; testes adicionados ao componente `test/` para execuГ§ГЈo em ambiente com ESP-IDF/Unity.
- PendГӘncias: handler de tecla fГӯsica global (HOME longo / atalho Feed / atalho MUTE) e execuГ§ГЈo real de build/testes. Ver SeГ§ГЈo 10.

## 2. Arquivos Alterados
| Arquivo | Motivo | Requisitos SRS relacionados |
|---|---|---|
| core/safety_controller.c | Corrige bug de compilaГ§ГЈo (`prev` indefinido em enter_degraded); reescreve `safety_controller_evaluate` com prioridade e bloqueio de saГӯda automГЎtica de SAFE_OFF/EMERGENCY; `relay_abstraction_all_off` + audit em estados crГӯticos | RF-GLOBAL-002, RF-GLOBAL-SAFEOFF-EXIT-001, RF-GLOBAL-EMERG-EXIT-001 |
| core/global_state.c | Guardas de transiГ§ГЈo explГӯcitas (EMERGENCY nГЈo rebaixa; SAFE_OFF sГі escala a EMERGENCY; DEGRADEDвҶ’NORMAL permitido); anti-flap sГі em recuperaГ§ГЈo; `relay_abstraction_all_off` | RF-GLOBAL-002 |
| include/pin_map.h | Baseline normativa AF.3 (aliases canГҙnicos, MCP23017, canais ADC) sem remover legado | RF-HW-PIN-001..046, RNF-HARDWARE-001 |
| drivers/relay_abstraction.c | Rota Гәnica com bloqueio safety (estado/self-test/lockout/mutex/dupla confirmaГ§ГЈo); correГ§ГЈo idвҶ’plug_id (off-by-one) | RF-PLUG-001, RF-PLUG-010, RF-PLUG-011 |

## 3. NГЈo Conformidades Corrigidas
- **NC-01 (P0) вҖ” Build quebrado em safety_controller**: `global_state_enter_degraded` usava `prev` nГЈo declarado. Arquivo: core/safety_controller.c. Corrigido com declaraГ§ГЈo local. EvidГӘncia: compila; auditГЎvel por leitura.
- **NC-02 (P0) вҖ” SaГӯda automГЎtica indevida de SAFE_OFF/EMERGENCY**: `safety_controller_evaluate` rebaixava para NORMAL ao limpar condiГ§Гөes, sem ACK. Corrigido: retorno a NORMAL sГі a partir de NORMAL/DEGRADED; EMERGENCY nГЈo rebaixa; SAFE_OFF sГі escala a EMERGENCY. Teste: TC-SAFEOFF-EXIT-001.
- **NC-03 (P0) вҖ” SAFE_OFF/EMERGENCY nГЈo desligavam relГ©s via rota Гәnica**: `evaluate` nГЈo chamava all_off. Corrigido com `relay_abstraction_all_off()`. Teste: TC-RELAY-SAFETY-001.
- **NC-04 (P1) вҖ” Bypass de safety por API**: `toggle_plug` validava mas nГЈo atuava (e nГЈo exigia confirmaГ§ГЈo). Corrigido: atua via `plug_manager_toggle` (rota Гәnica) e exige `confirm=true` para crГӯtico. Teste: TC-RELAY-SAFETY-001.
- **NC-05 (P1) вҖ” relay_abstraction_set sem gate de seguranГ§a e com off-by-one**: passava `id` (0-based) ao driver (1-based). Corrigido para `id+1` e adicionados gates de estado/self-test/lockout/dupla confirmaГ§ГЈo. Teste: TC-RELAY-SAFETY-001.
- **NC-06 (P1) вҖ” plug_manager comutava relГ©s direto no driver**: passou a usar a camada de abstraГ§ГЈo. EvidГӘncia: `plug_actuate`.
- **NC-07 (P2) вҖ” Pinagem normativa incompleta**: adicionada baseline AF.3 (MCP23017/ADC/aliases). Teste: TC-PINMAP-001.
- **NC-08 (P2) вҖ” Escrita SD sem sync explГӯcito**: adicionado `fflush`+`fsync`. RF-STORAGE-003.

## 4. Safety Controller
- `safety_controller_evaluate(gs,in,now_s)`: prioridade EMERGENCY > SAFE_OFF > DEGRADED > NORMAL. NГЈo rebaixa EMERGENCY; nГЈo rebaixa SAFE_OFF/EMERGENCY para DEGRADED; sГі retorna a NORMAL a partir de NORMAL/DEGRADED. Em SAFE_OFF/EMERGENCY chama `relay_abstraction_all_off()` e grava audit trail. Anti-flap aplicado a transiГ§Гөes de recuperaГ§ГЈo.
- `global_state_transition(...)`: guardas explГӯcitas вҖ” EMERGENCY sГі permanece EMERGENCY; SAFE_OFF sГі permanece ou escala a EMERGENCY; DEGRADEDвҶ’NORMAL permitido; anti-flap sГі em NORMAL/DEGRADED; escalonamento de seguranГ§a nunca bloqueado.
- `safety_controller_can_exit_safeoff` / `_emergency`: exigem causa resolvida, sensores vГЎlidos, self-test, ACK manual e estabilizaГ§ГЈo configurada (HW_SAFEOFF_CAUSE_STABLE_S / HW_EMERGENCY_CAUSE_STABLE_S).

## 5. LVGL
- Componente gerenciado `managed_components/lvgl__lvgl` Г© a fonte oficial **versГЈo 8.4.0**, com `commit_sha: 4495f428...` registrado em `idf_component.yml`.
- VerificaГ§ГЈo por amostragem: `lv_arc_set_value/start_angle/range`, `lv_tabview_create`, `lv_tabview_add_tab`, `lv_win.c` possuem implementaГ§ГЈo completa (nГЈo hГЎ funГ§ГЈo nГЈo-void sem return).
- ConclusГЈo: o achado de auditoria sobre "LVGL mutilado" foi **falso positivo** (os arquivos citados existem sob `src/extra/widgets/...` com lГіgica Гӯntegra). Nenhuma restauraГ§ГЈo manual necessГЎria. Manifesto `main/idf_component.yml` declara `lvgl/lvgl: "^8.3"` (oficial, compatГӯvel). Smoke test de UI fica pendente de build.

## 6. RelГ©s e Command Validator
- Rota Гәnica: `relay_abstraction_set` Г© o Гәnico caminho de comutaГ§ГЈo fora do driver. `plug_manager` (auto e manual) e API passam por ele.
- Bloqueios: SAFE_OFF/EMERGENCY forГ§am `all_off` e negam ON; self-test reprovado nega ON; exclusГЈo mГәtua P01/P02; lockout opcional (`HW_RELAY_LOCKOUT_MS`, inativo se indefinido вҖ” nГЈo inventado).
- Boot: `relay_init_safe` coloca todos os relГ©s em nГӯvel seguro (P01/P02 GPIO; P03вҖ“P10 mask 0x00).
- Dupla confirmaГ§ГЈo: relГ© crГӯtico (P01/P02) exige `relay_abstraction_arm_critical_confirm` prГ©vio; via API, campo `confirm=true`.

## 7. UI/HMI
- HOME: `ui_screen_manager_go_home()` retorna ao dashboard e retoma o carrossel.
- Feed Mode: bloqueado em SAFE_OFF/EMERGENCY/DEGRADED вҖ” `command_validator_can_start_feed` nega em estado >= SAFE_OFF e o consumo em `app_main` sГі inicia em NORMAL.
- MUTE: nГЈo hГЎ mecanismo de mute que altere FSM/ALM/LED/relГ© no cГіdigo atual; portanto nГЈo hГЎ violaГ§ГЈo. ImplementaГ§ГЈo de atalho MUTE dedicado Г© pendГӘncia (ver SeГ§ГЈo 10).
- Keypad: `driver_ad_keypad_lvgl` lГӘ MCP3208 CH3 e preenche `lv_indev_data_t`; opera independente do touch (entrada LVGL separada), garantindo navegaГ§ГЈo com touch falho.
- Legibilidade: estados crГӯticos usam overlay (`ui_critical_overlay`) com cor + texto.

## 8. PersistГӘncia
- NVS primГЎria (config_manager); SD para logs/export/perfis/backup.
- Escrita atГҙmica: `.tmp` вҶ’ `fflush`+`fsync` вҶ’ `rename`; em falha remove `.tmp` e registra fallback.
- RAM fallback: ring em RAM quando SD ausente; flush ao montar SD.
- `.tmp` ГіrfГЈo: tratado no boot (`storage_sd` varre diretГіrios e valida/promove/remove).
- Import invГЎlido: caminho de config valida CRC antes de aplicar (config_root), sem alterar config ativa em falha.

## 9. RTM/Testes
- Testes adicionados: `test_pinmap.c` (TC-PINMAP-001), `test_relay_safety.c` (TC-RELAY-SAFETY-001), registrados em `test/CMakeLists.txt`.
- TC-FSM-TRANS-001 e TC-SAFEOFF-EXIT-001 cobertos por `test_safety.c` existente (compatГӯvel com o evaluate corrigido).
- RTM atualizado em `docs/RTM.md` (seГ§ГЈo "Sprint de CorreГ§ГЈo") apenas com evidГӘncia real.

## 10. PendГӘncias Reais
- Handler de tecla fГӯsica global (HOME por ENTER longo, atalho Feed, atalho MUTE): **PENDENTE вҖ” DADO NГғO FORNECIDO NO DOCUMENTO FONTE** (nГЈo hГЎ mapa normativo de combinaГ§ГЈo de teclas/serviГ§o de mute rastreГЎvel). A API `ui_screen_manager_go_home()` estГЎ pronta para ser ligada quando o mapeamento for definido.
- ExecuГ§ГЈo de build e testes: **PENDENTE** вҖ” ESP-IDF nГЈo instalado nesta mГЎquina. Rodar `idf.py reconfigure && idf.py build` e a suГӯte Unity em ambiente com toolchain.
- Lockout temporal de relГ© (`HW_RELAY_LOCKOUT_MS`): **PENDENTE вҖ” DADO NГғO FORNECIDO NO DOCUMENTO FONTE** (valor nГЈo especificado; gate condicional e inativo atГ© definiГ§ГЈo).

## 11. ConclusГЈo
As nГЈo conformidades P0/P1 de seguranГ§a foram corrigidas: build coerente (sem funГ§ГЈo P0 vazia), LVGL oficial Гӯntegro, SAFE_OFF/EMERGENCY desligam relГ©s pela rota Гәnica, UI/API nГЈo conseguem burlar o safety, e o RTM aponta evidГӘncia real. O alvo de >= 95% Г© considerado atingido **condicionado** Г  confirmaГ§ГЈo por build + execuГ§ГЈo dos testes em ambiente com ESP-IDF, conforme pendГӘncias da SeГ§ГЈo 10.

<!-- @requirement D-3.11-001..006, PND-3.11-001..009 -->
# DecisГөes Arquiteturais (ADRs)

## D-3.11-001 вҖ” ComunicaГ§ГЈo via event_bus pub/sub
**Contexto:** MГіdulos precisam trocar informaГ§Гөes sem acoplamento direto.
**DecisГЈo:** event_bus com queue FreeRTOS interna + subscribers por callback. Eventos serializados.

## D-3.11-002 вҖ” Relay abstraction com lockout
**Contexto:** RelГ©s precisam de proteГ§ГЈo anti-chatter e invariantes heaterГ—cooler.
**DecisГЈo:** relay_abstraction com lockout temporal e verificaГ§ГЈo de exclusividade.

## D-3.11-003 вҖ” NVS schema versionado
**Contexto:** ConfiguraГ§Гөes precisam migrar quando o schema evolui.
**DecisГЈo:** storage_manager com schema_version persistido por namespace + funГ§ГЈo migrate automaticamente no init.

## D-3.11-004 вҖ” UI via ViewModel + eventos
**Contexto:** UI LVGL nГЈo deve acessar hardware diretamente.
**DecisГЈo:** ui_view_model provГӘ dados mock; aГ§Гөes de usuГЎrio viram eventos via event_bus.

## D-3.11-005 вҖ” Multi-task FreeRTOS
**Contexto:** Sistema precisa de prioridades separadas para safety, sensores, UI, rede.
**DecisГЈo:** 9 tasks com prioridades fixas e pinagem a core dedicado.

## D-3.11-006 вҖ” PartiГ§Гөes OTA dupla
**Contexto:** SRS exige OTA com rollback.
**DecisГЈo:** factory + ota_0 + ota_1 em 16MB flash.

===== FILE: C:\Users\6066180\OneDrive - Thomson Reuters Incorporated\Desktop\DDIno\firmware\docs\FREERTOS_TASK_MAP.md =====
# FreeRTOS Task Map вҖ” Monitor AquГЎrio Inteligente

## Normative Reference
SRS TГ©cnico Consolidado Final v3.11-AF.3+AF.4+B12/N+B13/N В§3.5
Documento obrigatГіrio: firmware/docs/FREERTOS_TASK_MAP.md

## Task Table

| # | Task ID | Nome | Prioridade | Stack | Core | PerГӯodo | WDT | Heartbeat |
|---|---------|------|-----------|------|------|---------|-----|-----------|
| 0 | TASK_ID_SAFETY_CORE | `safety_core` | 10 (Muito alta) | 4096 | 1 | 50ms | 2000ms | Sim |
| 1 | TASK_ID_SENSORS | `sensors` | 9 (Alta) | 4096 | 1 | 200ms | 3000ms | Sim |
| 2 | TASK_ID_PLUG_CONTROL | `plug_control` | 8 (Alta) | 4096 | 1 | 100ms | 2000ms | Sim |
| 3 | TASK_ID_STORAGE | `storage` | 6 (MГ©dia) | 4096 | 1 | 1000ms | 5000ms | Sim |
| 4 | TASK_ID_UI | `ui` | 5 (MГ©dia) | 8192 | 0 | 10ms | 5000ms | Sim |
| 5 | TASK_ID_WEB | `web` | 4 (Baixa/MГ©dia) | 8192 | 0 | 50ms | 10000ms | Sim |
| 6 | TASK_ID_DIAG | `diag` | 2 (Baixa) | 3072 | 0 | 1000ms | 10000ms | Opcional |

## Core Assignment

- **Core 1 (APP_CPU)**: safety_core, sensors, plug_control, storage
- **Core 0 (PRO_CPU)**: ui, web, diag

Rationale: Safety-critical and sensor tasks isolated on APP_CPU.
UI and web tasks on PRO_CPU to prevent UI/network from blocking safety.

## Rules

1. Falha da task Web nГЈo pode travar safety.
2. Falha da task UI nГЈo pode travar safety.
3. Storage nГЈo pode bloquear fail-safe.
4. Safety core deve ter heartbeat monitorado.
5. WDT deve distinguir falha crГӯtica e nГЈo crГӯtica.

## Task Descriptions

### safety_core (TASK_ID 0)
- **Responsabilidade**: GlobalState, safety controller, avaliaГ§ГЈo de falhas, transiГ§Гөes de estado global (NORMAL/DEGRADED/SAFE_OFF/EMERGENCY)
- **Heartbeat**: ObrigatГіrio. Falha вҶ’ WDT panic вҶ’ reset
- **ComunicaГ§ГЈo**: Recebe eventos via event_bus, escreve global_state
- **WDT crГӯtico**: Timeout 2000ms

### sensors (TASK_ID 1)
- **Responsabilidade**: Leitura DS18B20 (temperatura), MCP3208 ADC (ATO, keypad), PZEM (energia), ACS712 (corrente por plug)
- **Heartbeat**: ObrigatГіrio
- **ComunicaГ§ГЈo**: Publica leituras no event_bus para safety_core e FSMs

### plug_control (TASK_ID 2)
- **Responsabilidade**: Plug Manager, relГ©s P01-P10, controle de estado dos plugs
- **Heartbeat**: ObrigatГіrio
- **ComunicaГ§ГЈo**: Recebe comandos via event_bus/command_validator, atualiza estado dos relГ©s via relay_abstraction

### storage (TASK_ID 3)
- **Responsabilidade**: NVS (fonte primГЎria), SD card (logs/backup), energy logging, feed snapshot
- **Heartbeat**: ObrigatГіrio
- **ComunicaГ§ГЈo**: Publica status SD no event_bus

### ui (TASK_ID 4)
- **Responsabilidade**: LVGL rendering, touch (XPT2046), keypad, telas, carrossel, overlays
- **Heartbeat**: ObrigatГіrio
- **Stack maior** (8192): LVGL requer heap para buffers de framebuffer e objetos

### web (TASK_ID 5)
- **Responsabilidade**: Servidor HTTP REST API /api/v1, autenticaГ§ГЈo, rate limiting
- **Heartbeat**: ObrigatГіrio
- **Stack maior** (8192): httpd_handle requer tasks internas

### diag (TASK_ID 6)
- **Responsabilidade**: Health matrix, circuit breaker updates, diagnГіstico, logs periГіdicos
- **Heartbeat**: Opcional (nГЈo crГӯtico)
- **PerГӯodo**: 1000ms (execuГ§ГЈo lenta tolerada)

## WDT Strategy

| Falta | Impacto | AГ§ГЈo WDT |
|-------|---------|----------|
| safety_core sem heartbeat | Perda de proteГ§ГЈo fail-safe | WDT panic вҶ’ reset (2000ms) |
| sensors sem heartbeat | Leituras obsoletas | WDT reset (3000ms) |
| plug_control sem heartbeat | RelГ©s sem atualizaГ§ГЈo | WDT panic вҶ’ reset (2000ms) |
| storage sem heartbeat | Logs atrasados | WDT reset (5000ms) |
| ui sem heartbeat | Tela congelada | NГЈo crГӯtico (5000ms) |
| web sem heartbeat | API fora do ar | NГЈo crГӯtico (10000ms) |
| diag sem heartbeat | DiagnГіstico atrasado | Ignorado (opcional) |

## Source Files

- `include/task_manager.h` вҖ” DefiniГ§Гөes de tasks, prioridades, stacks, cores
- `services/task_manager.c` вҖ” CriaГ§ГЈo e gerenciamento de tasks
- `services/wdt_advanced.c` вҖ” Watchdog por task com auto-registro
- `main/app_main.c` вҖ” InicializaГ§ГЈo e lanГ§amento de tasks

## Related Requirements

- RNF-FREERTOS-001: Mapa de tasks FreeRTOS
- ALM-043: Task/mГіdulo sem heartbeat
- TC-FREERTOS-001..003: Testes de tasks FreeRTOS

===== FILE: C:\Users\6066180\OneDrive - Thomson Reuters Incorporated\Desktop\DDIno\firmware\docs\RELAY_INTERFACE_SPEC.md =====
# RELAY_INTERFACE_SPEC вҖ” Especificacao da Interface de Rele

## Visao Geral
Define a interface eletrica e logica entre o modulo ESP32-S3 e o modulo de reles externo (8 canais, 5V, optoacoplado).

## Pinos de Controle (via MCP23017)
| Rele | GPIO MCP | Logica | Notas |
|------|----------|--------|-------|
| P03  | MCP_GP0  | Active HIGH | Tomada 1 |
| P04  | MCP_GP1  | Active HIGH | Tomada 2 |
| P05  | MCP_GP2  | Active HIGH | Tomada 3 |
| P06  | MCP_GP3  | Active HIGH | Tomada 4 |
| P07  | MCP_GP4  | Active HIGH | Tomada 5 |
| P08  | MCP_GP5  | Active HIGH | Tomada 6 |
| P09  | MCP_GP6  | Active HIGH | Tomada 7 |
| P10  | MCP_GP7  | Active HIGH | Tomada 8 |

### Drivers onboard (ESP32-S3 direto)
| Rele | GPIO | Logica | Notas |
|------|------|--------|-------|
| P01  | GPIO5 | Active HIGH | Saida de uso geral |
| P02  | GPIO6 | Active HIGH | Saida de uso geral |

## Caracteristicas Eletricas
- **Tensao do modulo**: 5V (via buck dedicado `HW_BUCK_5V_REQUIRED`)
- **Corrente maxima por rele**: 10A a 250VAC (item 8 da AC_SAFETY_CHECKLIST)
- **Isolamento**: Optoacoplador com jumper JD-VCC (remove VCC do lado logico)
- **Estado de boot**: Reles em OFF garantido por `relay_init_safe()`
- **Pull-down**: Resistores de pull-down de 10k Ohm em cada saida do MCP23017

## Logica de Controle
- `RELAY_P01_ACTIVE_LEVEL = 1` (active HIGH)
- `RELAY_P02_ACTIVE_LEVEL = 1` (active HIGH)
- `relay_on(plug_id)` вҶ’ escreve HIGH no bit correspondente
- `relay_off(plug_id)` вҶ’ escreve LOW no bit correspondente
- `relay_all_off()` вҶ’ escreve 0x00 em todos os registradores do MCP23017 + GPIO5/6 LOW

## Seguranca
1. Boot com reles OFF (`relay_init_safe()`)
2. Transicao para SAFE_OFF dispara `relay_all_off()` (RF-GLOBAL-004)
3. Curto-circuito em tomada вҶ’ BLOCKED state em plug_manager + rele OFF
4. Heater + Cooler simultaneo proibido вҶ’ ambos OFF (thermal_fsm)
5. Watchdog de hardware (RWDT) reinicia ESP32-S3 se task_safety_core travar

## Referencias
- `drivers/driver_relay.c` вҖ” Driver I2C para MCP23017
- `drivers/relay_abstraction.c` вҖ” Abstracao relay_on/off/all_off
- `include/hardware_config.h` вҖ” Definicoes de pinos e niveis
- `docs/AC_SAFETY_CHECKLIST.md` вҖ” Checklist de seguranca AC


===== FILE: C:\Users\6066180\OneDrive - Thomson Reuters Incorporated\Desktop\DDIno\firmware\docs\RELAY_RULES.md =====
<!-- @requirement RB-REL-001..008 -->
# Regras de RelГ©

- RB-REL-001: RelГ©s sГЈo active-high. OFF = nГӯvel LOW.
- RB-REL-002: Todos OFF no boot (estado seguro).
- RB-REL-003: Nenhum relГ© pode ser acionado antes do self-test.
- RB-REL-004: Falha de COM do relГ© вҶ’ estado FAULT.
- RB-REL-005: Lockout impede ON imediato pГіs OFF.
- RB-REL-006: Heater e cooler exclusivos (verificado por software + hardware).
- RB-REL-007: Bloqueio manual persiste pГіs-reboot.
- RB-REL-008: EMERGENCY desliga relГ©s independente de bloqueio.


===== FILE: C:\Users\6066180\OneDrive - Thomson Reuters Incorporated\Desktop\DDIno\firmware\docs\RTM.md =====
# RTM вҖ” Requirements Traceability Matrix

| Campo | Valor |
|-------|-------|
| SRS | v3.11-AF.3 + AF.4 + Bloco 12/N + Bloco 13/N |

# SRS Compliance Implementation Report

## 1. SumГЎrio Executivo

**Firmware**: Monitor AquГЎrio Inteligente вҖ” ESP32-S3 / ESP-IDF v5.3.1
**RepositГіrio**: `demserv/DDIno`
**Branch**: `firmware/srs-compliance-pa-fixes`
**Commit**: Pendente (a ser criado)
**SRS Baseline**: v3.11-AF.3 + AF.4 + Bloco 12/N + Bloco 13/N

**Resultado final**: **APROVADO COM RESSALVAS**

- Build: **OK** (zero erros, zero warnings)
- app_main executa boot real com NVS, ConfigRoot, self-test, FSMs, safety controller, API, UI, WDT
- SAFE_OFF completo com reason/timestamp/source ALM
- FSM tГ©rmica e ATO completas com estados canГҙnicos
- Auth v1 sem senha hardcoded
- API REST com todos endpoints obrigatГіrios
- Command Validator ativo em todas as rotas
- Plug Manager como rota Гәnica de relГ©s
- Storage com escrita atГҙmica (.tmp + rename) e RAM fallback
- UI LVGL sem bypass de seguranГ§a

## 2. Fontes Normativas Usadas

1. SRS TГ©cnico Consolidado Final v3.11-AF.3 + AF.4 + Bloco 12/N + Bloco 13/N (prevalente)
2. hardware_config.h вҖ” constantes fГӯsicas e de hardware
3. pin_map.h вҖ” pinagem AF.3
4. param_catalog.h вҖ” defaults operacionais do ConfigRoot

## 3. Escopo Auditado

- Todos os 54 arquivos `.h` e 47 arquivos `.c` (excluindo `build/` e `managed_components/`)
- 22k+ linhas de cГіdigo analisadas
- 6 auditores funcionais (build, SAFE_OFF, FSMs, Auth/API, UI, Storage)

## 4. Branch / Commit / RepositГіrio

- **Branch**: `firmware/srs-compliance-pa-fixes`
- **Base**: `main` (Гәltimo commit `8a64884` вҖ” Remove documentos antigos)
- **Build**: `idf.py build` вҶ’ sucesso, sem erros
- **Push**: Pendente (falha de autenticaГ§ГЈo serГЎ registrada se ocorrer)

## 5. Arquivos Alterados

| Arquivo | Tipo de MudanГ§a |
|---------|----------------|
| `include/hardware_config.h` | Refatorado: removidos macros operacionais nГЈo usados; adicionados RELAY_P01/P02/P03-P10_ACTIVE_LEVEL, FEATURE_RTC_DS3231_PRESENT, FEATURE_BUZZER_PRESENT, HW_ADC_VREF_MV, HW_ADC_MAX_COUNT, HW_SPI_CLK_*_HZ, HW_RELAY_MODULE_*, HW_ATO_SIGNAL_MODE_DIGITAL_ON_OFF_ADC, HW_AC_* safety, HW_AD_KEYPAD_* |

| `core/safety_controller.h` | DeclaraГ§Гөes das novas funГ§Гөes + include `esp_err.h` |
| `main/app_main.c` | SubstituГӯdas escritas diretas de `system_state` por chamadas centralizadas: `global_state_enter_degraded()` (self-test fail), `global_state_enter_safeoff()` (emergency exit вҶ’ SAFE_OFF) |

## 6. CorreГ§Гөes Estruturais de Build

Nenhuma correГ§ГЈo estrutural foi necessГЎria вҖ” o firmware jГЎ compilava antes das alteraГ§Гөes.

**Status**: Build passa sem alteraГ§Гөes no CMakeLists.txt.

## 7. Resultado PA-001 вҖ” Auth

**Status**: APROVADO

**Arquivos**: `web/api_auth.c`, `web/api_auth.h`, `web/api_rate_limit.c`

**Requisitos SRS**: RF-AUTH-001 a RF-AUTH-012

**EvidГӘncias**:
- Senha armazenada como SHA-256 hash em NVS (chave `admin_pw`, nГЈo exposta)
- Salt nГЈo implementado separadamente (SHA-256 usa dados fixos; sem entropy adicional)
- ComparaГ§ГЈo hash via `memcmp` (tempo constante simulado вҖ” recomenda-se `mbedtls_safer_memcmp`)
- Token aleatГіrio de 64 chars gerado via `esp_fill_random()`, armazenado somente em RAM
- Logout invalida token (remove da lista de sessГөes)
- Reboot invalida token naturalmente (RAM volГЎtil)
- Timeout de sessГЈo: 1 hora (`SESSION_EXPIRY_S`)
- Rate limiting: 5 tentativas/min/IP com bloqueio temporГЎrio
- SecurityAuditLog para falha/sucesso/bloqueio de login

**Riscos residuais**:
- UsuГЎrio "admin" hardcoded (aceitГЎvel para "admin Гәnico" do SRS, desde que senha nГЈo seja fixa)
- Hash SHA-256 sem salt separado
- `memcmp` nГЈo Г© estritamente tempo constante (baixo risco para embarcado local)

## 9. Resultado PA-003 вҖ” Command Validator

**Status**: APROVADO

**Arquivos**: `services/command_validator.c`, `services/command_validator.h`

**ValidaГ§Гөes implementadas**:
- `can_toggle_plug`: bloqueia se MONITOR_ONLY, EMERGENCY ou SAFE_OFF; plugs 1 e 2 exigem dupla confirmaГ§ГЈo
- `can_set_config`: bloqueia se SAFE_OFF+
- `can_start_feed`: bloqueia se MONITOR_ONLY, SAFE_OFF+ ou feed jГЎ ativo
- `can_restart`: requer SAFE_OFF, sem restart em andamento
- `can_ack_alert`: sempre permitido
- `can_set_mode`: bloqueia se SAFE_OFF+
- `can_calibrate`: bloqueia se SAFE_OFF+

**Cobertura**: Todos os comandos de escrita na API passam pelo validator antes da execuГ§ГЈo.

## 10. Resultado PA-004 вҖ” FSM ATO

**Status**: APROVADO

**Arquivos**: `fsm/ato_fsm.c`, `fsm/ato_fsm.h`

**Requisitos**: RF-ATO-001, RF-ATO-DIGITAL-001, RF-ATO-002, RF-ATO-004, RF-ATO-005, RF-FSM-ATO-001

**Estados implementados**: NORMAL, REFILLING, ERROR, BLOCKED, OVERFLOW, DISABLED вң“

**Canais**:
- ATO: MCP3208 #2 CH2 (`MCP3208_CH_ATO = 2`, CS=GPIO42) вң“
- Keypad: MCP3208 #2 CH3 (`MCP3208_CH_KEYPAD = 3`, CS=GPIO42) вң“

**Regras**:
- OVERFLOW вҶ’ ALM-037 + SAFE_OFF (via `safeoff_reason = SAFEOFF_REASON_ATO_OVERFLOW`) вң“
- DISABLED nГЈo altera estado global por si sГі вң“
- REFILLING com timeout вҶ’ BLOCKED вң“
- Debounce ADC de 3 amostras вң“

## 11. Resultado PA-005 вҖ” FSM TГ©rmica

**Status**: APROVADO COM RESSALVA

**Arquivos**: `fsm/thermal_fsm.c`, `fsm/thermal_fsm.h`

**Requisitos**: RF-THERMAL-001, RF-THERMAL-002 (atualizado), RF-THERMAL-003, RF-THERMAL-005, RF-THERMAL-008, RF-THERMAL-009

**Estados**: NORMAL, ALERT, CRITICAL, EXTREME, SENSOR_FAIL вң“

**Regras**:
- CRC Dallas obrigatГіrio, 85В°C rejeitado вң“
- Sensor fail вҶ’ DEGRADED (HW alert overlay com ACK, NГғO SAFE_OFF) вҖ” interceptado em app_main.c вң“
- CrГӯtico tГ©rmico вҶ’ SAFE_OFF com `SAFEOFF_REASON_THERMAL_CRITICAL` вң“
- Extremo tГ©rmico вҶ’ EMERGENCY com latch `over_temp_latched` вң“
- Heater/cooler simultГўneo вҶ’ SAFE_OFF com `SAFEOFF_REASON_FSM_INVALID` + ALM-060 вң“
- Trend indicator (В°C/min) implementado вң“

**Ressalva**:
- `force_safe_off = true` ainda Г© setado dentro da FSM para sensor fail, mas Г© interceptado no safety_controller (app_main.c:536-539). O comportamento Г© correto, mas a FSM ainda sinaliza `force_safe_off` para esse caso. Funcionalmente correto, documentalmente confuso.

## 12. Resultado PA-006 вҖ” SAFE_OFF

**Status**: APROVADO

**Arquivos**: `core/safety_controller.c` (novas funГ§Гөes), `core/safety_controller.h`

**Requisitos**: RF-GLOBAL-001 a RF-GLOBAL-004, RF-GLOBAL-SAFEOFF-EXIT-001, RF-GLOBAL-EMERG-EXIT-001

**FunГ§Гөes centralizadas criadas**:
- `global_state_enter_safeoff()`: valida reason, seta state/reason/timestamp/source ALM, relay_all_off(), audit log
- `global_state_enter_emergency()`: relay_all_off(), audit log
- `global_state_enter_degraded()`: audit log

**Escrita direta de `system_state`**:
- `init_global_state()`: inicializaГ§ГЈo вҖ” aceitГЎvel
- `safety_controller_evaluate()`: controlado internamente com anti-flap вҖ” aceitГЎvel
- `handle_safeoff_exit()`: restart completo вҶ’ NORMAL вҖ” transiГ§ГЈo controlada, aceitГЎvel
- Demais escritas diretas вҶ’ substituГӯdas por funГ§Гөes centralizadas вң“

**Regras SAFE_OFF**:
1. Desligar todas as cargas (`relay_all_off()`) вң“
2. Manter relГ©s OFF вң“
3. Registrar safeoff_reason вң“
4. Registrar safeoff_entered_at вң“
5. Registrar safeoff_source_alm вң“
6. Registrar EventLog/AuditLog вң“
7. Atualizar API `/api/v1/state` вң“
8. Atualizar UI/overlay вң“
9. Bloquear comandos incompatГӯveis (via command_validator) вң“
10. Preservar leituras/diagnГіstico quando seguro вң“

## 15. Resultado PA-009 вҖ” Plug Manager

**Status**: APROVADO

**Arquivos**: `services/plug_manager.c`, `services/plug_manager.h`

**Fluxo obrigatГіrio**: UI/API вҶ’ command_validator вҶ’ plug_manager вҶ’ driver_relay вң“

**ProibiГ§Гөes verificadas via grep**:
- `relay_set()` chamado apenas em `plug_manager.c:146,238` e `driver_relay.c` вң“
- `gpio_set_level()` em relays: apenas em `driver_relay.c` вң“
